<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herzien.html>herzien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">revise, review</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

<ol><li>revision</li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:herziening.html>herziening</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***hes.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hes.html>hes</a> (64775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From either <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hesse.html>Hesse</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hessian.html>Hessian</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (possibly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hessenkiel</i>), or <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Häsz</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hesz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clothing, dress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hes.html>hes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hes.html>hessen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hesje.html>hesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A short, protective type of <a href = vnd.unilang:blouse.html>blouse</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:shirt.html>shirt</a>, typically worn by manual laborers</li>
<li>A light version of the above, worn as a signal, notably to be noticed by traffic</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Mostly used in its diminutive form (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hesje.html>hesje</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hässlich</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hateful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hes.html>hes</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hes.html>hesser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hes.html>hes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">hest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hesselijk</i></span></span>, <b><span class="Latn" lang="nl">heslijk</span></b></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***het.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> (4)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> contracted to <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a></i> in usual speech. This form <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> interpreted as being the same as the neuter pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> (etymology 2, see below), which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> contracted in the same way. This then <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> to the modern form/spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, which some might see as being unetymological.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>the <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the neuter definite article</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>the</b> book</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>the</b> girl</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">it</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*it</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>it; <span class="use-with-mention">third-person singular, neuter, subjective</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beetje.html>beetje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>It</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a nice house, but a little small.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>it; <span class="use-with-mention">third-person singular, neuter, objective</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>Kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>Can you see <b>it</b> well?</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> do <b>it</b> if you want <b>it</b>. (i.e. "if you want <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to")</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:honger.html>honger</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>geef</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boterham.html>boterham</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>The girl <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hungry, give her a sandwich.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>it; <span class="use-with-mention">impersonal</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>It</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> late.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:regent.html>regent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alweer.html>alweer</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><b>It'</b>s raining again.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b>?</i>
<dl><dd>How <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>it</b> going?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.</li>
<li>In a double-object construction with another pronoun, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally the direct object but precedes the other pronoun: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Give it back to him!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare regional English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Give it him back!</i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> different from other neuter pronouns, which usually follow the indirect object: <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Give that back to him!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:persoonlijk.html>Persoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b>
</p>

***heteluchtballon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heteluchtballon.html>heteluchtballon</a> (92520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lucht.html>lucht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ballon.html>ballon</a></i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***heten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heten.html>heten</a> (2864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hētan</i>, originally from the passive voice of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haitaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heten.html>heten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be named; to have as name; to be called.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:felix.html>Felix</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>This cat <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <a href = vnd.unilang:felix.html>Felix</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be (a translation or synonym of); to be called.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frans.html>Frans</a>?</i>
<dl><dd>What <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> that in French?</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To name, to call <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to provide with a name, to define a name as</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<ul><li><b>1900</b>, Frederik <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Eeden, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koele.html>koele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meren.html>meren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doods.html>Doods</a></i>, W. Versluys (publ., 1st ed.), page 7.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>Haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> Hedwig Marga <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Fontayne.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>call</b> her name Hedwig Marga <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Fontayne.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be <a href = vnd.unilang:claimed.html>claimed</a>; to be asserted.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziek.html>ziek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In a lot of dialects and colloquially the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noemen.html>noemen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">call, give a name</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi"><a href = vnd.unilang:heten.html>heten</a></i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally considered incorrect<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not usually tolerated in written Dutch.</li></ul>

***heu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> heu (19196)</h1><br></body> 
***heugen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heugen.html>heugen</a> (29281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huegen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huggen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hugjaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">think, consider</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The geminate <i>-gg-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> simplified through influence from the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huege</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heugen.html>heug</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heugen.html>heugen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remain in one's memory</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remind</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:heugen.html>heugen</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:onpersoonlijk.html>onpersoonlijk</a></span> in <a href = vnd.unilang:geheugen.html>geheugen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijblijven.html>bijblijven</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heugen.html>heugen</a></b>!" <a href = vnd.unilang:sprak.html>sprak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dreigend.html>dreigend</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***heul.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heul.html>heul</a> (64770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hole</i>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heul.html>heul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heulen.html>heulen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heul.html>heultje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A floodgate with a bridge.</li>
<li>A stone or brick bridge, usually consisting of only a single arch.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sewer or a ditch for wastewater.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> possibly obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A temporary bridge, often made of wood.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*huel</i>, attested in compounds corresponding to modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">heulzaad</i>, from older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">oleum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heul.html>heul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:poppy.html>poppy</a>, plant of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:papaver.html>Papaver</a></i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">klaproos</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">maankop</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papaver.html>papaver</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> several <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of soporific <a href = vnd.unilang:drugs.html>drugs</a> made from the <a href = vnd.unilang:poppy.html>poppy</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">maankop</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:papaver.html>papaver</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">slaapbol</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">slaapkruid</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something soothing, healing, salutary or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> redeeming.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a></span></li></ul>

***heur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heur.html>heur</a> (92513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A dialectal variation of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> used predominantly in Groningen.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heur.html>heur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">personal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> her. Sometimes (though decreasingly) used in Standard Dutch, especially in poetry and in conjunction with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> (in the sense of <i>hair</i>), for the sake of euphony or comic effect.
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:heur.html>Heur</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weelderig.html>weelderig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a>.
<dl><dd><b>Her</b> luxuriant hair.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***heus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heus.html>heus</a> (1371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hovesch</i>, and thus the same word as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hoofs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">courtly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>For the semantic and phonetic development of this word compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hübsch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pretty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language">Central Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">höösch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">careful, slow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heus.html>heus</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heus.html>heuser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heus.html>heus</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heust</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>friendly, polite</li>
<li>real, genuine</li>
<li>impressive for being indistinguishable from the real thing; nothing less than...
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:komende.html>Komende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaterdag.html>zaterdag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lokaal.html>lokaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omgetoverd.html>omgetoverd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heus.html>heuse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:discotheek.html>discotheek</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>You <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> believe it, but next Saturday, the hall (of our youth movement) will be transformed into a real discotheque.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***heuvel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heuvel.html>heuvel</a> (3380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hoevel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huevel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hovel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huffel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">huvil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hubilaz</i>. Cognate with dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hübel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Hiwwel</i>. Related with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hȳf</i> (modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></i>). <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hevich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hevig.html>hevig</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habīgaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">six angles</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hexagon</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aal</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hexagonal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hexagonal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hexagonal</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hibiscus.html>hibiscus</a> (105472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:hibiscus.html>hibiscus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hibiscum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἰβίσκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ibískos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marsh mallow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably ultimately from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span> language such as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hibiscus.html>hibiscus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hibiscuses</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hibisci</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A flower of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hibiscus.html>Hibiscus</a></i>, especially <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hibiscus.html>Hibiscus</a> syriacus</i>, found in tropical to temperate regions, of some species used for making infusions/tea.</li>
<li>A cocktail made with <a href = vnd.unilang:champagne.html>champagne</a> and cranberry juice.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***hick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hick.html>hick</a> (129610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hick.html>Hick</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pet form of Richard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hick.html>hick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hicks.html>hicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An awkward, naive, clumsy and/or rude country person. <span class="defdate">[from early 18th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boor.html>boor</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">country bumpkin</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">churl</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hillbilly.html>hillbilly</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lob.html>lob</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:redneck.html>redneck</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">rustic</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">yokel</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hick.html>hick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hicks.html>hicks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hiccup</li></ol>
</body> 
***hickey.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hickey.html>hickey</a> (82785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hickey.html>hickey</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hickeys</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bruise-like mark made during petting by pressing the mouth to the skin on one’s partner’s body and sucking. <span class="defdate">[from 1934]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">love bite</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">lovebite</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">knot</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An object whose name <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown or cannot be recalled. <span class="defdate">[from 1909]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A printing defect caused by foreign matter on the printing surface resulting in a <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> where the ink <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing, appearing as a spot of ink surrounded by a halo, or as an unprinted spot within a solid printed area.</li>
<li>Local swelling in a tissue area, especially skin, often due to injury. <span class="defdate">[from 1915]</span></li>
<li>A tool for making smooth, semicircular bends in conduit and pipe.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">conduit <a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> business<span class="ib-comma">,</span> finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unintended negative outcome or loss in regards to a deal or action, often preceded by the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> "taking a ..." or "<a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> a ... ".
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Farmer Jones <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hickey.html>hickey</a></b> on his soybean crop when the flood washed the seeds away.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***hickory.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hickory.html>hickory</a> (57255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A shortening of <i>pockerchicory</i>/<i>pokickery</i>/<i>pohickery</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from an <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algonquian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Algonquian languages">Algonquian</a></span></span> language, probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ojibwe_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ojibwe language">Ojibwe</a></span>/<span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algonquin_language" class="extiw" title="w:Algonquin language"><a href = vnd.unilang:algonquin.html>Algonquin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="alq">pawcohiccora</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hickory.html>hickory</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of or pertaining to the <a href = vnd.unilang:hickory.html>hickory</a> tree or its wood.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hickory.html>hickory</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hickories</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various deciduous hardwood trees of the genus <i>Carya</i> or <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Annamocarya" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Annamocarya"><i>Annamocarya</i></a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The wood of these trees.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hickory.html>hickory</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  
</p>
<ol><li><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/carya" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:carya"><span style="color:green;"><i>carya</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:botanische.html>botanische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hout.html>hout</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslacht.html>geslacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> okkernootfamilie <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Juglandaceae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Juglandaceae"><span style="color:green;"><i>Juglandaceae</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /></li></ol>

***hier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> (32)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hē₂r</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>here</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> this</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:aanwijzen.html>aanwijzend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>bijwoord</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:nabij.html>nabij</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></i>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a>!</b> (</i><a href = vnd.unilang:uitroep.html>uitroep</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:klein.html>klein</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a><i>)</i> </li>
<li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goud.html>goud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevonden.html>gevonden</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> locatief <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> voornaamwoordelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>bijwoord</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervangt.html>vervangt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanwijzen.html>aanwijzend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:nabij.html>nabij</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a></b> </i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></b>)<i> </i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i>`<b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:links.html>links</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vindt.html>vindt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a>  <a href = vnd.unilang:bibliotheek.html>bibliotheek</a>;  <a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gids.html>gids</a>, '<a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarachter.html>daarachter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>groene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaal.html>zaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Chinese <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Grand_Hotel_Europa,_p._15_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Grand_Hotel_Europa,_p._15-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a> (10412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hiernamaels</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hereafter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">namaals</i>. Originally an adverb.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaalsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaalsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">afterlife</span>, life after death</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hereafter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">afterwards</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of or relating to the afterlife.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>

***hii.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hii.html>hii</a> (116825)</h1><br></body> 
***hij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> (15)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hie.html>hie</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><i>Third-person singular, masculine, subjective:</i> he.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:loopt.html>loopt</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>He</b> walks.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>When the word occurs other than as the first word of a clause and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not emphatically stressed, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually pronounced as <span class="IPA">/i/</span>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a completely accepted pronunciation in standard speech.
</p>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a>.</i> </li>

***hijsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hijsen.html>hijsen</a> (12458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hisen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hischen</i>. Further etymology uncertain, but possibly related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hatjaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hunt down, pursue, persecute, attack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Or, possibly imitative.
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">hissen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hissen</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hil</a> (64763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hil</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hille</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulliz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stone, rock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kolən-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*koləm-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">top, hill, rock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hill</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hullen.html>hulle</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">hull</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">hóll</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">holm</i>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">hilarité</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hilaritās</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheerfulness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hilaris</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheerful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + noun of state <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-tās</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱλαρός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hilarós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
